So not making petrol and diesel doesn't mean we'll stop using oil.   And no matter what the more economical stable countries do, the poor ones will always keep destroying more than we can fix. Good old Bandvagn 206! It's not a "Swedish" version on anything though, it's a Swedish design that's been exported all over the world. In use by the US Army and Marines, UK, Spain and dozens of others. The Sisu Nasu is a later 80s "clone" produced, entirely new design that just looks similar to a 206. By that point the Finns had been using the 206 for decades, little brother always with his copying ;)

I apologize in advance for this rant, but it is something that I have to do as a truly homeless person. I will start this of with saying that i enjoy watching your videos. Now what I have to say is that you are miss representing what true homelessness is except where you were talking about Dave living in the office at some of your locations. True homelessness is where a person or small family has no place to live. I know this from personal experience as I am currently living in a homeless shelter. Your business being ' homeless' is another thing all together as many businesses when first starting out are are in the same position. They might start out in a small storage unit and then as they start to grow the will move to some place with a bigger footprint. Many businesses will do this till they finally get big enough that they have to buy a big enough piece of land to have as a premiant location with room to expand. Now that I have said that here is b brief explanation where I am coming from. I have worked hard ALL my life till about 4 years ago when I became unable to work any more do to old injuries and my girlfriend becoming unable to fully take care of her self which left me having to use up the money that was in my saving up till the day she died. This left me living in my van just parking where ever I could with having to go into public bathrooms to clean up everyday at one of the city parks. This continued on till I was finally able to get into a local homeless shelter where I'm at now.
